<s> it is a pretty room with white panelled walls and chrysanthemums and carmine lilies in bowls <\s>
<s> a large bow window overlooks the park under a sou' westerly sky <\s>

<s> doors opposite each other lead to the maid's workroom and to a corridor <\s>

<s> well freda suppose you just give it up <\s>
<s> i don't like to be beaten <\s>
